Unfortunately, the biggest failure was the "extremely noisy" and "noisy" sound of the large water pump machine outside the hotel window! I've been suffering from it all night!
From the moment you enter the room until you leave the room, the high-decibel sound of large machines running makes your whole head feel buzzing and painful! Logically speaking, in a building as high as the 14th floor, such a "noisy" noise should not be so clear, but it is true that the quality of a night's sleep is seriously affected by it. As soon as the window is opened, I want to breathe, but I don't know what's going on. "Deafening"! It is conceivable that if you are a guest living on a "lower floor", you will probably feel like you are being "attacked by a bomber"!
Therefore, for the few five-star hotels in Nanqiao Old Town with good reputations for many years, the hotel should give "serious attention" to this issue. Guests pay to have a rest, not to suffer such "noise pollution"! Low-quality sleep gives guests a very bad experience! I hope the person in charge of the hotel can live up to the "five-star" brand at the front desk and solve the "environmental pollution" around it as soon as possible! Whether it is the use of large machines, coordinating with them to adopt "staggered peak opening", or using other feasibility study methods to prevent "noise pollution" from poisoning hotel guests, it is a need for a long-established "five-star hotel" Provide a solution and a reasonable explanation and statement to the customer!
